    75	
    76	def recommended_next_action(
    77	    slug: str,
    78	    state: dict | None,
    79	    stages: dict[str, dict[str, object]],
    80	    reconciliation_ok: bool,
    81	) -> str:
    82	    if state is None:
    83	        state = load_workflow_state(slug)
    84	    blocked = state.get(BLOCKED_KEY, {})
    85	    if blocked.get("active"):
    86	        return "mark_blocked"
    87	    discovery = state.get(DISCOVERY_KEY, {})
    88	    if blocking_unresolved_items(discovery) or (discovery.get("required") and not discovery.get("complete")):
    89	        return "discover"
    90	    if _judge_panel_needed(state):
    91	        return "judge_panel"
    92	    stages_state = state.get("stages") or {}
    93	
    94	    def _judge_advanced(stage_name: str) -> bool:
    95	        """FR-001 — honor the judge panel's formal advance verdict.
    96	
    97	        When judges voted advance, downstream behavior treats the stage as
    98	        ready to hand off even if the artifact SHA has drifted since the
    99	        last checkpoint. factory_cmd_checkpoint reseals the manifest lazily
   100	        (FR-002) so the next checkpoint starts from a clean manifest.
   101	        """
   102	        stage_blob = stages_state.get(stage_name) or {}
   103	        return stage_blob.get("judge_next_action") == "advance"
   104	
   105	    if not stages["spec"]["artifact_exists"] or not stages["spec"]["artifact_meaningful"]:
   106	        if later_progress_exists(stages, "spec")[0]:
   107	            return "mark_blocked"
   108	        return "author_spec"
   109	    if not _judge_advanced("spec") and (
   110	        not stages["spec"]["manifest_exists"] or not stages["spec"]["healthy"]
   111	    ):
   112	        return "repair_spec_checkpoint"
   113	    if not stages["plan"]["artifact_exists"] or not stages["plan"]["artifact_meaningful"]:
   114	        if later_progress_exists(stages, "plan")[0]:
   115	            return "mark_blocked"
   116	        return "author_plan"
   117	    if not _judge_advanced("plan") and (
   118	        not stages["plan"]["manifest_exists"] or not stages["plan"]["healthy"]
   119	    ):
   120	        return "repair_plan_checkpoint"
   121	    if not stages["tasks"]["artifact_exists"] or not stages["tasks"]["artifact_meaningful"]:
   122	        if later_progress_exists(stages, "tasks")[0]:
   123	            return "mark_blocked"
   124	        return "author_tasks"
   125	    parallel = state.get(PARALLEL_ANALYSIS_KEY, {})
   126	    if not parallel.get("reviewed"):
   127	        return "record_parallel_analysis"
   128	    if not _judge_advanced("tasks") and (
   129	        not stages["tasks"]["manifest_exists"] or not stages["tasks"]["healthy"]
   130	    ):
   131	        return "repair_tasks_checkpoint"
   132	    if not stages["diff"]["artifact_exists"]:
   133	        return "dispatch_next_slice_to_codex"
   134	    if not stages["diff"]["manifest_exists"] or not stages["diff"]["healthy"]:
   135	        return "repair_diff_checkpoint"
   136	    if diff_review_budget_state(slug).get("head_mismatch"):
   137	        return "repair_diff_checkpoint"
   138	    if not reconciliation_ok:
   139	        return "reconcile_reviews"
   140	    # If any tasks remain unchecked there are more slices to implement before delivering.
   141	    tasks_path = workflow_dir(slug) / "tasks.md"
   142	    if tasks_path.exists() and "- [ ]" in tasks_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"):
   143	        return "dispatch_next_slice_to_codex"
   144	    # Import here to avoid circular — refresh_delivery_snapshot is in factory_deliver
   145	    from factory_deliver import refresh_delivery_snapshot  # noqa: E402
   146	    delivery = refresh_delivery_snapshot(state.get(DELIVERY_KEY, {}))
   147	    if not delivery.get("pr_url"):
   148	        return "deliver"
   149	    if delivery.get("head_mismatch"):
   150	        return "deliver"

    85	def _ensure_stage_state_blob(state: dict, stage: str) -> dict:
    86	    stages = state.setdefault("stages", {})
    87	    stage_state = stages.get(stage)
    88	    if not isinstance(stage_state, dict):
    89	        stage_state = {}
    90	    stage_state.setdefault("adversarial_rounds", 0)
    91	    stage_state.setdefault("judge_rounds", 0)
    92	    stage_state.setdefault("judge_verdicts", [])
    93	    stage_state.setdefault("annotations", [])
    94	    stage_state.setdefault("unresolved_concerns", [])
    95	    stage_state.setdefault("adversarial_sha_history", [])
    96	    stage_state.setdefault("initial_sha", "")
    97	    stages[stage] = stage_state
    98	    try:
    99	        schema_version = int(state.get("schema_version", 1))
   100	    except (TypeError, ValueError):
   101	        schema_version = 1
   102	    if schema_version < 2:
   103	        state["schema_version"] = 2
   104	    return stage_state
   105

   107	def _stage_int(stage_state: dict, key: str) -> int:
   108	    try:
   109	        return int(stage_state.get(key, 0) or 0)
   110	    except (TypeError, ValueError):
   111	        return 0
   112	
   113	
   114	def _judge_panel_payload_from_state(slug: str, state: dict) -> dict[str, object] | None:
   115	    stages = state.get("stages", {})
   116	    if not isinstance(stages, dict):
   117	        stages = {}
   118	    for stage in ("spec", "plan", "tasks", "diff", "closeout"):
   119	        stage_state = stages.get(stage, {})
   120	        if not isinstance(stage_state, dict):
   121	            stage_state = {}
   122	        adversarial_rounds = _stage_int(stage_state, "adversarial_rounds")
   123	        judge_rounds = _stage_int(stage_state, "judge_rounds")
   124	        judge_verdicts = stage_state.get("judge_verdicts", [])
   125	        latest_round = judge_verdicts[-1] if isinstance(judge_verdicts, list) and judge_verdicts else []
   126	        block_count = 0
   127	        if isinstance(latest_round, list):
   128	            for verdict in latest_round:
   129	                if isinstance(verdict, dict) and verdict.get("verdict") == "block":
   130	                    block_count += 1
   131	        if adversarial_rounds >= 3 and judge_rounds == 0:
   132	            return {
   133	                "next": "judge_panel",
   134	                "reason": f"{stage} reached adversarial round cap",
   135	                "blockers": [f"{stage}.adversarial_rounds >= 3"],
   136	            }
   137	        if judge_rounds < 3 and block_count >= 2:
   138	            return {
   139	                "next": "judge_panel",
   140	                "reason": f"{stage} judge panel voted block",
   141	                "blockers": [f"{stage}.judge_verdicts[-1] block-majority"],
   142	            }
   143	    return None
   144	
   145	
   146	def _checkpoint_next_action_payload(slug: str, state: dict, completed_stage: str) -> dict[str, object]:
   147	    stages = {stage: stage_manifest_state(slug, stage) for stage in CHECKPOINT_STAGES}
   148	    recon_ok, _ = reconciliation_state(slug)
   149	    next_action = recommended_next_action(slug, state, stages, recon_ok)
   150	    judge_panel_payload = _judge_panel_payload_from_state(slug, state)
   151	    if next_action == "judge_panel" and judge_panel_payload is not None:
   152	        return judge_panel_payload
   153	    return {
   154	        "next": next_action,
   155	        "reason": f"{completed_stage} checkpoint completed",
   156	        "blockers": [],
   157	    }
   158

   160	def _persist_last_action_result(slug: str, payload: dict[str, object]) -> None:
   161	    update_workflow_state(
   162	        slug,
   163	        lambda state: state.__setitem__("last_action_result", payload),
   164	    )

   167	def _rollback_adversarial_round(slug: str, stage: str) -> None:
   168	    state = load_workflow_state(slug)
   169	    stage_state = state.get("stages", {}).get(stage, {})
   170	    if not isinstance(stage_state, dict):
   171	        stage_state = {}
   172	    current_rounds = _stage_int(stage_state, "adversarial_rounds")
   173	    update_stage_state(
   174	        slug,
   175	        stage,
   176	        {"adversarial_rounds": max(current_rounds - 1, 0)},
   177	    )

   180	def command_checkpoint(args: argparse.Namespace) -> int:
   181	    fast = getattr(args, "fast", False)
   182	    if fast and args.stage != "diff":
   183	        raise SystemExit("--fast requires --stage diff")
   184	
   185	    ensure_sync()
   186	    root = workflow_dir(args.slug)
   187	    reviews = reviews_dir(args.slug)
   188	    root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   189	    reviews.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   190	
   191	    if not fast:
   192	        prereq_error = prerequisite_failure(args.slug, args.stage)
   193	        if prereq_error:
   194	            raise SystemExit(prereq_error)
   195	    if not fast and args.stage == "tasks":
   196	        parallel = load_workflow_state(args.slug).get(PARALLEL_ANALYSIS_KEY, {})
   197	        if not parallel.get("reviewed"):
   198	            raise SystemExit(
   199	                "tasks checkpoint requires parallel analysis first; "
   200	                "run 'parallel --slug <slug> --note \"...\"' to record whether "
   201	                "parallel implementation opportunities exist in tasks.md"
   202	            )
   203	    if not fast and args.stage == "spec":
   204	        discovery = discovery_state(args.slug)
   205	        blocking = blocking_unresolved_items(discovery)
   206	        if blocking:
   207	            if discovery_blockers_are_malformed(discovery):
   208	                raise SystemExit(
   209	                    "spec checkpoint requires discovery state to be repaired first; "
   210	                    "use discover --clear to reset malformed discovery state"

   238	def command_repair(args: argparse.Namespace) -> int:
   239	    from factory_cmd_checkpoint import command_checkpoint  # noqa: E402
   240	    ensure_sync()
   241	    state = load_workflow_state(args.slug)
   242	    stages = {stage: stage_manifest_state(args.slug, stage) for stage in CHECKPOINT_STAGES}
   243	    repaired: list[str] = []
   244	    notes: list[str] = []
   245	    blocked_reason = ""
   246	
   247	    print(f"workflow: {args.slug}")
   248	    print("repair:")
   249	
   250	    for stage in ["spec", "plan", "tasks", "diff"]:
   251	        stage_state = stages[stage]
   252	        drift = stage_drift_class(stage, stage_state)
   253	        _, orphaned = stage_review_inventory(args.slug, stage)
   254	        if stage_repairable(args.slug, stage, stage_state):
   255	            print(f"- {stage}: repairing {drift}")
   256	            result = command_checkpoint(repair_checkpoint_args(args.slug, stage, stage_state))
   257	            if result != 0:
   258	                blocked_reason = f"{stage} repair failed"
   259	                break
   260	            refreshed = stage_manifest_state(args.slug, stage)
   261	            stages[stage] = refreshed
   262	            if not refreshed["healthy"]:
   263	                blocked_reason = f"{stage} remains unhealthy: {trim_detail(str(refreshed.get('detail', '')))}"
   264	                break
   265	            repaired.append(stage)
   266	            if orphaned:
   267	                notes.append(f"{stage}: preserved {len(orphaned)} orphaned historical review file(s)")
   268	            continue
   269	
   270	        print(f"- {stage}: {stage_status_label(args.slug, stage, stage_state)}")
   271	
   272	        if drift in {"missing-artifact", "stub-artifact"} and later_progress_exists(stages, stage)[0]:
   273	            blocked_reason = f"{stage} has {drift.replace('-', ' ')} while later workflow material exists"
   274	            break
   275	        if drift == "unhealthy-manifest" and not stage_repairable(args.slug, stage, stage_state):
   276	            blocked_reason = f"{stage} checkpoint is not safely repairable: {trim_detail(str(stage_state.get('detail', '')))}"
   277	            break
   278	
   279	    if not blocked_reason:
   280	        # Repair closeout if manifest is stale (only when it exists and is unhealthy)
   281	        closeout_state = stages["closeout"]
   282	        closeout_drift = stage_drift_class("closeout", closeout_state)
   283	        if closeout_drift == "unhealthy-manifest" and stage_repairable(args.slug, "closeout", closeout_state):
   284	            print("- closeout: repairing unhealthy-manifest")
   285	            result = command_checkpoint(repair_checkpoint_args(args.slug, "closeout", closeout_state))
   286	            if result != 0:
   287	                blocked_reason = "closeout repair failed"
   288	            else:
   289	                refreshed = stage_manifest_state(args.slug, "closeout")
   290	                stages["closeout"] = refreshed
   291	                if not refreshed["healthy"]:
   292	                    blocked_reason = f"closeout remains unhealthy: {trim_detail(str(refreshed.get('detail', '')))}"
   293	                else:
   294	                    repaired.append("closeout")
   295	        elif closeout_drift == "unhealthy-manifest":
   296	            # unhealthy-manifest but not repairable — block so repair doesn't silently succeed
   297	            blocked_reason = "closeout is unhealthy but not repairable"
   298	        elif closeout_drift not in {"not-checkpointed", "missing-artifact", "stub-artifact"}:
   299	            print(f"- closeout: {stage_status_label(args.slug, 'closeout', closeout_state)}")
   300	
   301	    if blocked_reason:
   302	        print(f"- blocked: {blocked_reason}")
   303	        for note in notes:
   304	            print(f"- note: {note}")
   305	        return 1
   306	
   307	    recon_ok, recon_detail = reconciliation_state(args.slug)
   308	    next_action = recommended_next_action(args.slug, state, stages, recon_ok)
   309	    print("")
   310	    if repaired:
   311	        print(f"- repaired: {', '.join(repaired)}")
   312	    else:
   313	        print("- repaired: none")
   314	    if notes:
   315	        for note in notes:
   316	            print(f"- note: {note}")
   317	    if not recon_ok:
   318	        print(f"- follow-up: reconciliation still blocked ({trim_detail(recon_detail)})")
   319	    print(f"next-action: {next_action}")
   320	    return 0

codex
## Findings
- **Medium [CODE-CONFIRMED]**: FR-009 does not cover all state-mutating entry points. `run_factory.py` only post-checks `{"checkpoint", "judge", "reconcile", "auto-reconcile", "implement", "deliver", "block"}`, but `repair` and `closeout` are also user-facing commands and both mutate workflow state by calling `command_checkpoint()`. That leaves the new contradiction guard able to miss the same bad state on two important paths. [run_factory.py](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/friendly-aryabhata-9efbf7/docs/workflow/operations/codex-skills/feature-factory/scripts/run_factory.py#L102) [factory_cmd_status.py](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/friendly-aryabhata-9efbf7/docs/workflow/operations/codex-skills/feature-factory/scripts/factory_cmd_status.py#L238) [factory_cmd_deliver.py](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/friendly-aryabhata-9efbf7/docs/workflow/operations/codex-skills/feature-factory/scripts/factory_cmd_deliver.py#L473)

- **Medium [CODE-CONFIRMED]**: The invariant check is being evaluated against the wrong decision context. `_run_post_invariants()` hardcodes `recommended_next_action(..., True)`, while the real checkpoint path computes the next action from the actual reconciliation state. If reconciliation is blocked, the warning can be computed against a branch the user would never see, which makes the contradiction detector unreliable in edge states. [run_factory.py](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/friendly-aryabhata-9efbf7/docs/workflow/operations/codex-skills/feature-factory/scripts/run_factory.py#L116) [factory_cmd_checkpoint.py](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/friendly-aryabhata-9efbf7/docs/workflow/operations/codex-skills/feature-factory/scripts/factory_cmd_checkpoint.py#L146)

- **Medium [CODE-CONFIRMED]**: FR-005a splits the meaning of “resolved” from the code that already exists. The spec’s unresolved filter only excludes concerns with `addressed_at`, `deferred_reason`, or `dismissed_reason`, but `factory_pr_body.py` already treats `addressed_by` as enough to move a concern into the resolved block and prints that field as the resolution detail. A concern with only evidence attached will therefore be classified one way by the UI and another way by the spec’s filter. [factory_pr_body.py](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/friendly-aryabhata-9efbf7/docs/workflow/operations/codex-skills/feature-factory/scripts/factory_pr_body.py#L32) [factory_pr_body.py](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/friendly-aryabhata-9efbf7/docs/workflow/operations/codex-skills/feature-factory/scripts/factory_pr_body.py#L123)

- **Medium [CODE-CONFIRMED]**: The new concern lifecycle is not actually operable from the open-concerns view the spec preserves. `render_judge_panel_block()` prints stage, judge, confidence, reasoning, and round history for unresolved concerns, but it does not print the `id` that the proposed `--address`, `--defer`, and `--dismiss` flows need. Only the resolved-concerns block includes the ID, so operators still have to inspect `state.json` to recover it. [factory_pr_body.py](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/friendly-aryabhata-9efbf7/docs/workflow/operations/codex-skills/feature-factory/scripts/factory_pr_body.py#L93) [factory_pr_body.py](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/friendly-aryabhata-9efbf7/docs/workflow/operations/codex-skills/feature-factory/scripts/factory_pr_body.py#L117)

## Residual Risks
- Legacy `state.json` readers that bypass the shared loader can still miss the new defaulting behavior for `invariant_warnings` and concern fields. The spec assumes read-time normalization, but that only helps if every path actually uses the shared accessors.
- The regex fix is still format-bound. Any reviewer style that falls outside the anchored markdown shapes in FR-006 will remain invisible to `auto-reconcile` until someone adds a new pattern and a regression test.
